chain consists of multiple components located in the staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver module. The core admission framework is defined in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/, which provides the chainAdmissionHandler (chain.go) that chains multiple admission handlers together. The chain implements the Admit() and Validate() methods to sequentially process requests through admission handlers, returning immediately on the first error.\\n\\nThe webhook admission controller is implemented as a generic Webhook class (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go) that orchestrates webhook calls. This generic webhook is used by two concrete plugins: MutatingAdmissionWebhook (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go) and ValidatingAdmissionWebhook (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go).\\n\\nThe webhook dispatch logic is handled by separate dispatchers for mutating (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go) and validating (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go) webhooks. These dispatchers iterate through registered webhooks, determine if they should be called based on namespace selectors, object selectors, and rule matching, and then invoke the webhook via callAttrMutatingHook or similar methods.\\n\\nWebhook configurations are managed by configuration managers: mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go) and validatingWebhookConfigurationManager (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go). These managers maintain cached views of dynamic webhook configurations from the API server.\\n\\nThe webhook call dispatch uses WebhookAccessor (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go) to provide a common interface to both mutating and validating webhook metadata. The core admission framework is defined in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/, which provides the chainAdmissionHandler (chain.go) that chains multiple admission handlers together. The chain implements the Admit() and Validate() methods to sequentially process requests through admission handlers, returning immediately on the first error.\\n\\nThe webhook admission controller is implemented as a generic Webhook class (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go) that orchestrates webhook calls. This generic webhook is used by two concrete plugins: MutatingAdmissionWebhook (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go) and ValidatingAdmissionWebhook (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go).\\n\\nThe webhook dispatch logic is handled by separate dispatchers for mutating (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go) and validating (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go) webhooks. These dispatchers iterate through registered webhooks, determine if they should be called based on namespace selectors, object selectors, and rule matching, and then invoke the webhook via callAttrMutatingHook or similar methods.\\n\\nWebhook configurations are managed by configuration managers: mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go) and validatingWebhookConfigurationManager (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go). These managers maintain cached views of dynamic webhook configurations from the API server.\\n\\nThe webhook call dispatch uses WebhookAccessor (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go) to provide a common interface to both mutating and validating webhook metadata. Request/response handling is performed in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go, which handles creation of AdmissionReview objects and verification of webhook responses.\\n\\nAdmission response aggregation is performed in the dispatchers, particularly in the mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch() method, which processes webhook responses, applies patches from mutating webhooks, and handles reinvocation context when webhooks modify the object.\\n\\nPredicate matching logic is split across multiple files: namespace selector matching (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/predicates/namespace/matcher.go), object selector matching (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/predicates/object/matcher.go), and rule matching (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/predicates/rules/rules.go).
